3a1(ka'o): / min sangs/ thams cad dang 'byung nyid du los/ zhes gsungs pas/ de'i tshe 'dus pa'i tshogs kyis/ thams cad rgyu rkyen gyis ma skyes pas/ ye zhes rang snang du mthong /

3b1(ka'o): yang dag pa/ con nyid gsung dung sems la yod/ yon tan dkyil 'khor yang dag pa/ bon nyid gsung dung sems la yod/ 'phrin las dkyil 'khor yang dag pa/ bon nyid gsung drung 
3b2(ka'o): sems la yod/ de'i mtshan nyid gang zhes pa/ yang dag nges par dran par gyis/ sems kyi rang bzhin skye ba med/ sems kyi rang bzhin dngos po med/ sems kyi 'bras bu ma bcos pa// 
3b3(ka'o): sems kyi sku ni sangs rgyas pa/ sems kyi gsung ni btags pa yin/ sems kyis thugs ni go ba ste/ sems kyi yon tan zad med pa/ sems kyi 'phren las lhun grub pa/ nges /

4b1(ka'o): shes min/ lhun grub nyid la bcos med pas/ rtsol med skyes pa'i ye shes men/ nam mkha' lta bu'i ye shes la/ phyogs res med pa ye bdal pa/ lhun gyis grub pa'i /

4b6(ka'o): rang gsal gyi nar bzhag/ dran pa sems kyi mzhor zin/ de nyid tshogs drug lhug par bzhag/ m nor sems kyi slob dpen la/ lus don dran pas thag bcad cing / bsam med 
5a1(ka'o): dran med mi g.yo g/ m spyod legs pa'i don mi bzlung / bslu ba ma yin pro ba me/ me tog gsal ba ma bcos pa/ dul ba ma yin d pbyal ba'i/ reg pa de nyid

5a3(ka'o): mi bya/ shes pa ma bsdu yan du bkyi/ shes pa mi dgag zhan mi bya/ mtshan ma'i spro ba 'chal ba na/ sna tshogs rtogs pa'i sems byung na/ lus sems klod la gzer chen 
5a4(ka'o): gdab/ shin tu dran pa g.yog pa na/ stong nyid bde ba'i man ngag sbyin/ me re gsang ba'i dgongs pa la/ gang yang ma yin de ltar yin/ tha dad brtag par 'dzin pa dang / rol pa'i snang

8a3(ga'o): logg pa dang / tbon po mang poss gnhi gang / bdag la bstod cing bskor ba dang / mdung dar mang po sbyar ba dang / drag po dbal rom thar ba dang / glang chen non cing bo btab dang / 
8a4(ga'o): bla ma slob dpon lung ston dang / snang sred bran du 'khol ba dang / dngos sam nyams sam rmaMs las su/ mthun par snang zhing byung ba ni/ bsnyen pa grub pa'i rtags su bshad/ de tshe tang 
8a5(ga'o): 'dzin bstan pa yi/ yi dam lha gsal ting 'dzin sgom/ mchod bstod tshogs dang gtor ma dang / yo byad 'ban tshogs gser skyems bcas/ dus gsum mchod cing bstod pa 
8a6(ga'o): 'brul/ 'phrin las btsol zhing smon lam gdab/ gtor ma btang zhing man 'dal bsdu/ me ri 'd gsal 'phrin las kyi rgyud las/ bsnyen pa bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// 
8b1(ga'o): / de rjes sgrub pa bstan pa ni/ de yang phyi nang gsang ba gsum/ phye dus bkod pa lha gnas su/ sgrub pa'i thabs ni 'di ltar ro// bsnyen pa s+dzogs shing rtags cen nas/ dkyil / 
8b2(ga'o): 'khor zhal bsgyur 'phrin las brtsam/ dkyil 'khor 'dam gang gu bzhi la/ dpangs su khu gang yod pa brtsegs/ de la sman lnga rin chen lnga/ sogs lnga sbyar ba'i chag chag 
8b3(ga'o): gdab/ de nas cig gdab dkyil 'khor ni/ dbus su 'jig pa dmar ser la/ gong dang mthun pa'i man 'dal ni/ mtho gang tchad du gsum brtsigs bya/ dang po gser mdog de 'og 
8b4(ga'o): g.su/ de 'og phyogs dang btun par bya/ me ri gong dang mthun par bris/ de la mu khyud zlum pos bskor/ zla gam bzhi po ser po ba/ mu khyud dkar po g.yung drung mdzes/ de'i phyi rim 
8b5(ga'o): 'khor lo brgyad/ dmar ser me yi 'khor lo bra/ de la mu khyud zlum pos bskor/ mu khyud me re mdzes par bris/ gong ras dmar skug zur gsum pa/ gu chad mtsho bzhi ljang khur 
8b6(ga'o): bya/ bar khyams ser po glo 'byur dmar/ sgo dang lcags ra ldan pa yang / shin tu dod cing mdzes par bris/ sgrub pa rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor la/ dmigs pa'i pur pa lha ye sku/ dbus / 
9a1(ga'o): / su tzan dkar po 'am/ rgya hrug dkar la byas pa sM/ bur pa dkar po khru gang chad/ darg dkar cod pan btags pa cig/ ye zshes lha ra mnga' gsol la/ ba rim dang 
9a2(ga'o): po'i steng du gzug/ tan sdug po'i zhing dag gam/ 'o ma can gyi shing dag la/ phur pa 'dzub gang sor bzhi byas/ ljang khu dar gyi cod pan btags/ s+dzu 'phrul lha ru mnga' gsol 
9a3(ga'o): la/ bang rim bar ma'i steng du gzug/ gnam thags drag po'i thig thags sam/ mi bsad mtshen las byas pa yis/ pur pa 'dzub gang sor gnyis pa/ dmar ser dar gyi cod 
9a4(ga'o): pan btags/ sprul pa'i khro bar mnga' gsol la/ bang rim tha ma'i steng du gzug/ drug shing phur pa mtho gang tshad/ dar gyi cod pan riM re ldan/ yum gnyis dag du mnga' gsol 
9a5(ga'o): la/ sprul pa'i dbal chen g.yas g.yon gzug/ g.yas g.son zla gam gnyis po la/ gser gyi 'khor lo rtsebs brgyad la/ gdug pa'i shing la byas pa'i/ bur pa sor ni 
9a6(ga'o): bcu drug la/ dar gyi cod pan re re gdags/ yab yum nyi shur mnga' gsol la/ phyogs mtshams ma 'khrug gzug par bya'o// steng 'og zla gam gnyis po dang / gong ras gru 
9b1(ga'o): gsum gdan steng du / 'gug sgrol nyi su mnga' gsol la dgod/ dri dang kha dag ldan pa'i shing dag la/ pur pa rtsi ser bcu gnyis pa/ dar gyi cod pan re re gdags/ dmag dpon / 
9b2(ga'o): bzhi ru mnga' gsol lo// glo 'byur bzhi la dgod par bya'o// rin chen pur pa ser brgyad pa/ gyad chen bzhi ra mnga' gsol la/ cod pan gdags shing sgo bzhir dgod/ de'i phyi 
9b3(ga'o): rim bar khyams la/ gdug pa'i tshang dmar bcu gnyis la/ las mkhan bcu gnyis mnga' gsol kyang / de yi phyi ram rtsang dmar te/ gdug pa'i mtshon cha mi bsad las/ po / 
9b4(ga'o): nya bcu gnyis mnga' gsol dgod/ lhags re zangs re phyi mtha' la/ ti ka'i lha tshogs sum brgya drug cu dang / sman tshogs dgu khri dgu 'bum ryten/ nyungs dkar sgong shag re re 
9b5(ga'o): 'am/ brag mtsho' be'u ri res bskor/ dkyil 'khor bla yi steng rgyan du/ dar dmar ras la srel ba yi/ lo tso la ri nyi 'di res/ gyur re gdugs kyi tshul du prub/ bar rgyan me / 
9b6(ga'o): shel me long dang / gcan gzan mgo phreng mdzes par dgod/ me re 'di gsal 'phrin las kyi rgyud las/ sgrub pa'i dkyil 'khor dang / rgyan bcas bstan pa'i le'u ste drug pa'o// 
10a1(ga'o): / sgrub pa'i du s bsham pa'i rdang / bha rnam thag dam bskang bi khyi/ kbhun brag dng ma zhe / ses pu sh gam hadang / sheg lug gshin shad bca'/ 
10a2(ga'o): stag rgod g.yag rgod bya rgod dang / gzig rgod nya rgod las sogs pa'i/ sha khrag dbang po rnam lngar bcas/ gdung khrag mtshun khrag gsen khrag dang / zhal zas spyan gzigs 
10a3(ga'o): yo byad sogs/ 'ban pud gtor mar bcas pa rnams/ thugs dam bskang ba'i rdzas su bsags/ mar me tshan chab lha sangs sos/ 'bru dang me tog ma lus pa/ dkyil 'khor lha 
10a4(ga'o): la mchod phyir bsags/ mtshal yos gla ba chu gtsang dang / mkhan songs shugs pa yid du 'ong / dag cing gtsang ma'i s+dzas su bsags/ g.sag dkar lug dkar ra dkar dang / 
10a5(ga'o): g.sung du hugs pa rten du 'dzug/ gsung bsnyen dril bu bcas pa rnams/ dus gsum rgyun du mtchod phyir bshams/ mkhon dang tha rtsogs med par bya/ mi 'thing po dang yug s mo// 
10a6(ga'o): sdig can las sogs bsnyen mi bya/ drag po'i s+dzas su bsags pa ni/ dug zhing sna tshigs shing dag gam/ gdug pa'i cher nag shing dag la/ mgo 'dzug ldog la hom du thar/ byad 
10b1(ga'o): ma dang 'ug pa dang / klag gis sgron ba'i mda' dag la/ ser po dbar po sngon po gdags/ rtam shing nyid la btsug la bsgrub/ bdu g.sag rig po'i ra g.yas la/ rtsi mo khrag dang 
10b2(ga'o): btsag gis byug/ de yi kha la rgyan 'di gdags/ zhe sdang rno ba'i snying rtse dang / dgra la sa ba'i le rtse dang / snom pa sna yi 'dzengs gnyer dang / ltha ba mig gi 'bras bu dang / 'drel 
10b3(ga'o): psnga ma'i rtsi mo rnams/ ra yi kha la btags te bskor/ nang du gdug pa'i thun s+dzas gsal/ thun la hus gdab bsgrub par bya/ lu du rig po' ba g.yas su/ dgra bgegs 
10b4(ga'o): bzhan pa'i s+dzas rnams bshams/ me ro 'd gsal 'phren las kyi rgyud ces bya ba las/ sgrub pa'i s+dzas bshams pa'i le'u ste bdun pa'o// // de tche sngags kyi phreng ba 'di/ ma 
10b5(ga'o): yangs rgyun du bzlas par bya/ dang por ye shes lha yi sngags/ snying po 'di bzlas 'phro 'du bya/ nyi lo yo/ oM a hUM/ ha ra khaM khar re 'dushA/ de nas s+dzu 'dhrul lha yi snying po 'di / 
10b6(ga'o): bzlas/ 'phro 'du bya/ nye lo yo/ a ~M hUM/ ha ra khi khar re 'du dza/ de nas las kyi khro rgyal gyis/ sprul pa dbal chen ge khod la/ snying po 'di bzlas 'phro 'du bsgom/ 
11a1(ga'o): / b/ 'jig rten khams rnams dbang du sud/ nye lo yoi/ leg mur tshar gyi hir cha s/ khyim mdur shogs s spungs seM r/ gi khod so gs s spungs seM r/ g.yas nas skur 
11a2(ga'o): bskyed sgrol ba'i yum/ nam mkha'i o saus rgyal mo yis/ snying po 'di bzlas dgra bgegs bsgral/ nye lo yo/ danga ra mu ni ra/ len ge lo la ni/ g.yon na dgyes sgrol sbyor / 
11a3(ga'o): ba'i yum/ ne sus srid pa'i mnga' bdag mo'i/ snying po 'di bzlas thams cad 'gug/ nye lo yso/ ne sus ma ma tang khang len/ ge lo la ni/ phyogs bcu'i khro ba yab yum dang / 
11a4(ga'o): sprul pa 'gug sgrol nyi shu yi/ sngags rnams dring zhing 'phro 'du bya/ nye lo yo/ phya che na/ man tce na/ man zhags ce na/ gyer rgyung ce na/ 'breing gong rgyung ce na/ ge khod ngag 
11a5(ga'o): zhung ce na/ pra pud pud ce na/ pa bhur thur ce na/ tad ta tsaMs se na/ rkyail sud ce na/ dza rhad len/ ge lo le na de nas sgo ba gyad bzhi' sngags/ bar chad bzlog phyir drag tu 
11a6(ga'o): bzlas/ g yo khod d dresr pa / ge.yo khod da yag ma pa / ge.yo khod do na ga pa / ge yo khod d kla sa pa / de nas dmag dpon ma bzhi' sngags/ dpung bskyed dgra bgegs 'dul 
11b1(ga'o): byer bzlang / nye lo ye ma sa tang thams/ le bsu ni sung ting steng sas/ len ge lo la ni/ de nas las mcan bcu gnyig sngags/ las bni rdzogs par bya byer bzlang / te /

11b4(ga'o): ma ma tang rag sho stong kham rag stang rza ha/ de ltar sngags dang snying po rnams/ rab kyi chu bo'i gzhung lta bu/ me drag mi zhan mi bur bar/ bar chad 'gal 'khrul med par bzlas/

11b6(ga'o): grub rtags rab 'bring tha ma gsum/ rab ni dngos su 'byung ba ste/ 'bring ni nyams su ston pa yin/ tha ma mtshan lhas rmaM lam du / me chen 'bar dang nyi ma shar/ glog dmar 
11b7(ga'o): 'khyug dang tsha tsha 'phro/ thog dmar 'bab dang tsaM dmar 'phen/ bya gcan mang pos re log gang / bon po mang po'i khrom 'tshogs dang / rnga brtung gshang bkrol dung chen 'byud/ gtor 
12a1(ga'o): ma sdzas dang pur pa las/ me stag 'phro zhing 'di 'byung dang / drid dang rlang pa la sogs 'byung / me re 'd gsal 'phrin las kyi rgyud las/ bsgrub pa'i sngags dang rtags 
12a2(ga'o): bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// / de nas ting 'dzin rim pa la/ nyams su blang zhing bsgom pa'i don/ bdag nyid rig pa gsal stong nga/ je yang ma bsgrub stong pa las/ mi skye 
12a3(ga'o): mi 'gag gyer mi dmigs/ lhun grub chen por bdal pa'i ngang / de bzhin nyid du rnam par dag/ ye nas stong zhing bdag med la/ rmongs 'khrul gzung 'dzin log pa rnams/ tshaMd 
12a4(ga'o): med bzhi ye thugs rje yis/ kun la snyoms zhing bdal bar sgom/ rang nyid spul sku'i thugs ka nas/ a/ ya/ ra ba/ su lnga las/ 'od zer mthing nag ldang khu dang / dmar 
12a5(ga'o): po sngon po ser po dang lnga/ rim gyis 'bras bu dkyil 'khor gsal/ de steng yig 'bru rung ldan las/ kha daog lnga yis 'od zer 'bar/ de la ri rab lhun po nyid/ rin chen sna lnga'i 
12a6(ga'o): rgyu las grub/ zur bzhi log brgyad brjid par sgom/ gzi brjid re rab lhun po'i rtse/ steng mnyam yid 'ong mdzes pa ru/ bder gshegs sprul pa'i gzhal yas khang / kha dag 
12b1(ga'o): dbyibs legs blta na bsdug/ yangs shing rgya che tsan gyi dbyings/ phyogs mtshams rin chen 'bar bas mdzes/ nyams dga' yid 'ang phun sum tshogs/ yon tan bsam 'das 
12b2(ga'o): gu bzhir rgyas/ bon nyid dbyings chen rtsi mo zlum/ bkod legs bon gyi po brang sgom/ po brang bon gyi gzhal yas su/ ra la khrag gi rgya mtshar 'khyil/ kla la g.yen 
12b3(ga'o): dgu' thod chen gyi/ khre brtsigs rgya mtsho' gting nas blangs/ de steng yig 'bru thung a kha/ yi gid yis bon las/ gser gyi khyung chen ldeng ba dang / rlung gisnga mong mag dgu dang / 
12b4(ga'o): bse yir skyes khaM dkar gsum/ ram gyis gtso ba'i gdan du bskyed/ de nas khri gdan s+dzogs steng du/ yi ge dri yai sa bon las/ re ra ye zhes me 'di skur/ sbur bsdus dbal 
12b5(ga'o): chen ge khod gnyis/ dbu dgu phyag ni bco brgyad pa/ zhabs ni rnam pa drug du bsgrad/ btsa ma gser ltar kha dag gser/ gser gyi me stag tsha tsha 'pro/ ba spu'i bu ga thams 
12b6(ga'o): cad nas/ g.su ya du 'byur sprin lthar gtibs/ spyi gtsug gser gyi khyung chen lding / sku stod bdud srin g.yang gzhi la/ sku smad chu mo' pad rnams btags/ tbrul nag 
13a1(ga'o): gdug pa'i sku rig cing / grag go cig bzlog mche ba brtsigs/ shin tu 'jig sngam chas dgu brgyan/ bca brgyad gdug pa'i mtshen cha bsdam / sgu ci / 
13a2(ga'o): yan lag rag par bsgom/ dbu gtsug nyi zla pad ma'i steng / yi ge a dkar rgya skar mdog/ 'phro 'du ye zhes lha ya sku/ sku mdog dkar gsal zhal dkar mdog/ rang bzhin 
13a3(ga'o): phyag rgya lnga dang ldan/ mtshan dang dpe byad yongs su s+dzogs/ a te mu kher gsal bar sgom/ thugs kar nyi zla pad ma'i steng / yig 'bru o nyid sna tshogs 'od/ sblar bsdus sdu 
13a4(ga'o): 'pul lha ye sku/ zhi ba'i nang gi brkyang bskum tshul/ g.yas pas gser gyi chags shing la/ rin chen g.su yi g.sung drung can/ g.yin pas brda' yi phyag rgya can/ ku byi 
13a5(ga'o): mang ke thugs kar sgom/ mgon po rnam gsum s+dzogs pa'i sku/ gzi brjid ye zhes me 'di 'bar/ las dang nyon mongs bsregs par sgom/ g.yas su yi ge ma nyid las/ sgrol 
13a6(ga'o): yul o slas rgyal mo nyid/ dmar nag zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ me shel 'bum gyi ral pas brgyan/ khro chu'i phur pa 'driel bar bsgom/ g.yon pas gser 'od mu nyid 
13b1(ga'o): la/ sbyor yum ni slas rgyal mo nyid/ ser nag zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ g.yas pas yab 'khyud he thun stobs/ g.yon pas khrag zhal yab la 'brul/ rin chen gser / 
13b2(ga'o): gye ral bas brgyan/ yab sum gnyis su med par sgom/ de nas gtso mo yab sum gyi/ thugs ka'am zni sbyor 'tshams nas/ yi ge dri r dag la ni/ 'di 'phres bdag gzhan 
13b3(ga'o): don byas te/ khro ba bcu dang khro mo bcug/ 'jigs tshul ngam chen 'bar bar bskyed/ dza dang ra gyi sa bon las/ 'gug sgrol nyi snu s+dzogs par bskyed/ po nya bcu gnyis kla las 
13b4(ga'o): bskyed/ dmag dpon ma bzhi man chad dang / ti ka'i lha 'khor sum brgya rnams/ 'jig rten las la grub pa ste/ rang rgyud pa yi lha yin pas/ sa bon spro bsdu mi dgos te/ 
13b5(ga'o): chu las nya ldang tshul du bskyed/ ting 'dzin dkyil 'khor gsal ba yis/ lha rnams s+dzogs par sku bskyed do// me re 'od gsal 'phrin las kyi rgyud las sgrub pa'i ting 'dzin 
13b6(ga'o): bstan pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// // de nas gyer spungs bsgrub pa pos/ ye shes dbyings nas grub pa'i lha/ thugs rje 'gro ba'i don mdzad rnams/ me rie 'od dpung gzhal yas su/ 
14a1(ga'o): / b/ mgon po rnam gsum s+dzogs pa'i lha/ yab yum gnyis med 'khrel sbyor tshul/ thabs dang shes rab rol pa las/ khro bo khro mo'i sprul pa dang / las mkhan po nya / 
14a2(ga'o): 'thar bcas rnams/ dam tshig gnas su spyan rangs shing / gus pa'i lus dang gdung ba'i ag/ brtse ba'i sems kyis gus phyag 'tshal/ bskyed pa'i dkyil 'khor gnal yas du/ 
14a3(ga'o): mgon po rnam gsum gtso 'khor bcas/ dgyes pa'i tshul gyis bzhugs su gsol/ ji ltar mgon po' lha spyed ltar/ de bzhin sgub gnhin gyer sungs kyis/ sad kher dkyil

14a6(ga'o): than mong mchod pa rnam lnga 'brul/ thun mong ma yin pa yi s+dzas/ bdud rtsi sman gyi mchod pa 'bul/ dug gsum rgyud las grol ba'i s+dzas/ ha khrag rus gsum mchod pa / 
14b1(ga'o): 'brul/ gzung yul bhyi la ma chags shing / 'dzin pa'i yid gnyis rang grol ba'i/ sbyor dang sgrol ba'i mchod pa 'brul/ thugs dam longs spyod chen po' brgyan/ dbang po lnga yi / 
14b2(ga'o): spyod yul du/ 'doid yin lnga yi longs spyod phyir/ zhal zas tshogs kyi mchod pa 'brul/ de nas lha rnams snyan gsan dbab/ longs spyod tshogs kyi smon lam gdab/ bdag 
14b3(ga'o): gi sku gsum s+dzogs pa yi/ sku gsung thugs kyi sngags 'dzab drings/ grub rtags rab 'bring tha ma gsum/ rab ni dngos grub 'byung ba ste/ 'bring gi nyams su myong ba yin/ tha mas 
14b4(ga'o): mtshan ltas dag tu 'byung / sku dang ye shes rol pa'i rgyan/ gyad pur gsang ba'i dkyil 'khor lha/ thugs nyid rnam dag dgongs pa yis/ bstod cing bskul la 'phrin las bcol/

14b6(ga'o): thun 'pong zer gyi las bya zhing / cha gcig bsreg la cha gcig mnan/ cha gcig pud dang rab sbyar la/ gtor mar btab cing gtang rag 'brul/ de nas gtor ma byin gyis / 
15a1(ga'o): rlabs/ bhag ma'i tsho gs+dzogs pa dang / pa 'baba lhadang brten mala/ gbyer ung gnhen gyi sbyings lbyen/ dkyil 'thor bsa zhi lha rnam pyo// pha gsang / 
15a2(ga'o): skyabs shing bkra shes brjod/ gtang rag dbul zhing ston mo dgye/ de nas gyir spungs gnhen rab kyis/ lha dang dkyil 'khor bdag nyid gsum/ rig pa'i 'd dpung gcig tu 'drel//

15a6(ga'o): b'am/ yang na pur bu dar ba'i dus/ thrul lam phag gi nyi ma'am/ gza' skar nyi ma gdug pa la/ drag po'i las 'jug sbyor ba tsam/ ci ltar 'tshams pa gdon mi zad

15b6(ga'o): gur du dbub/ de nas dgra gzugs ling ka ni/ dri ma rkang rjes phyi sa dang / skra dang gos kyi dum bu dang / bdud chad lnga las gzugs byas la/ kho rang cag 'dra'i kha dag bsgyur/ gro 
16a1(ga'o): glazhi shan / ra khri lhal ni blon ta byo/ 'khri nyi ska blon da byo/ bdgcrig lzlan rog/ nye ska smg ra se bko/ 'gug gtsag/
